# <a name="troubleshoot-aspnet-core-on-azure-app-service-and-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-103">Risolvere i problemi relativi a ASP.NET Core in app Azure servizio e IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-103">Troubleshoot ASP.NET Core on Azure App Service and IIS</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-104">Di [Justin Kotalik](https://github.com/jkotalik)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-104">By [Justin Kotalik](https://github.com/jkotalik)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-105">Questo articolo fornisce informazioni sugli errori comuni di avvio delle app e istruzioni su come diagnosticare gli errori quando un'app viene distribuita in app Azure servizio o IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-105">This article provides information on common app startup errors and instructions on how to diagnose errors when an app is deployed to Azure App Service or IIS:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-109">Fornisce consigli per la risoluzione dei problemi per le app distribuite nel servizio app Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-109">Provides troubleshooting advice for apps deployed to Azure App Service.</span></span>

[<span data-ttu-id="b43de-110">Risolvere i problemi in IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-110">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>](#troubleshoot-on-iis)  
<span data-ttu-id="b43de-111">Fornisce consigli per la risoluzione dei problemi per le app distribuite in IIS o in esecuzione in IIS Express localmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-111">Provides troubleshooting advice for apps deployed to IIS or running on IIS Express locally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-112">Le linee guida sono valide per le distribuzioni di Windows Server e Windows desktop.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-112">The guidance applies to both Windows Server and Windows desktop deployments.</span></span>

## <a name="app-startup-errors"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-117">Errori di avvio dell'app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-117">App startup errors</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-118">In Visual Studio, per impostazione predefinita, un progetto ASP.NET Core viene [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) host durante il debug.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-118">In Visual Studio, an ASP.NET Core project defaults to [IIS Express](/iis/extensions/introduction-to-iis-express/iis-express-overview) hosting during debugging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-119">Un errore *502,5-Process* o un *errore di avvio 500,30* che si verifica quando il debug locale può essere diagnosticato utilizzando i consigli in questo argomento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-119">A *502.5 - Process Failure* or a *500.30 - Start Failure* that occurs when debugging locally can be diagnosed using the advice in this topic.</span></span>

### <a name="40314-forbidden"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-120">403,14 non consentito</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-120">403.14 Forbidden</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-121">Non è possibile avviare l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-121">The app fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-122">Viene registrato l'errore seguente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-122">The following error is logged:</span></span>

```
The Web server is configured to not list the contents of this directory.
```

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-123">L'errore è in genere causato da una distribuzione interruppe sul sistema host, che include uno degli scenari seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-123">The error is usually caused by a broken deployment on the hosting system, which includes any of the following scenarios:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-124">L'app viene distribuita nella cartella errata del sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-124">The app is deployed to the wrong folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-125">Il processo di distribuzione non è riuscito a spostare tutti i file e le cartelle dell'app nella cartella di distribuzione nel sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-125">The deployment process failed to move all of the app's files and folders to the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-126">Il file di *web.config* non è presente nella distribuzione oppure il contenuto del file di *web.config* non è valido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-126">The *web.config* file is missing from the deployment, or the *web.config* file contents are malformed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-127">Effettuare i passaggi seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-127">Perform the following steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-128">Eliminare tutti i file e le cartelle dalla cartella di distribuzione nel sistema di hosting.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-128">Delete all of the files and folders from the deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-129">Ridistribuire il contenuto della cartella di *pubblicazione* dell'app nel sistema host usando il normale metodo di distribuzione, ad esempio Visual Studio, PowerShell o la distribuzione manuale:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-129">Redeploy the contents of the app's *publish* folder to the hosting system using your normal method of deployment, such as Visual Studio, PowerShell, or manual deployment:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-130">Verificare che il file *web.config* sia presente nella distribuzione e che il relativo contenuto sia corretto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-130">Confirm that the *web.config* file is present in the deployment and that its contents are correct.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-131">Quando si esegue l'hosting in app Azure servizio, verificare che l'app venga distribuita nella `D:\home\site\wwwroot` cartella.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-131">When hosting on Azure App Service, confirm that the app is deployed to the `D:\home\site\wwwroot` folder.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-132">Quando l'app è ospitata da IIS, verificare che l'app venga distribuita nel **percorso fisico** IIS visualizzato nelle impostazioni di **base** di **Gestione IIS**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-132">When the app is hosted by IIS, confirm that the app is deployed to the IIS **Physical path** shown in **IIS Manager**'s **Basic Settings**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-133">Verificare che tutti i file e le cartelle dell'app vengano distribuiti confrontando la distribuzione nel sistema di hosting con il contenuto della cartella di *pubblicazione* del progetto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-133">Confirm that all of the app's files and folders are deployed by comparing the deployment on the hosting system to the contents of the project's *publish* folder.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-134">Per ulteriori informazioni sul layout di un'app ASP.NET Core pubblicata, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-134">For more information on the layout of a published ASP.NET Core app, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-135">Per ulteriori informazioni sul file di *web.config* , vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-135">For more information on the *web.config* file, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#configuration-with-webconfig>.</span></span>

### <a name="500-internal-server-error"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-136">500 - Errore interno del server</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-136">500 Internal Server Error</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-137">L'app viene avviata, ma un errore impedisce al server di soddisfare la richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-137">The app starts, but an error prevents the server from fulfilling the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-138">Questo errore si verifica all'interno del codice dell'app durante l'avvio o durante la creazione di una risposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-138">This error occurs within the app's code during startup or while creating a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-139">La risposta potrebbe non avere alcun contenuto o essere visualizzata nel browser come un codice *500 Errore interno del server*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-139">The response may contain no content, or the response may appear as a *500 Internal Server Error* in the browser.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-140">Il log eventi dell'applicazione in genere indica che l'app è stata avviata normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-140">The Application Event Log usually states that the app started normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-141">Dal punto di vista del server, questo è corretto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-141">From the server's perspective, that's correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-142">L'app è stata effettivamente avviata, ma non può generare una risposta valida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-142">The app did start, but it can't generate a valid response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-143">Per risolvere il problema, eseguire l'app dal prompt dei comandi nel server o abilitare il log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-143">Run the app at a command prompt on the server or enable the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log to troubleshoot the problem.</span></span>

### <a name="5000-in-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-144">500.0 Errore di caricamento del gestore in-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-144">500.0 In-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-145">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-145">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-146">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-146">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-147">Si è verificato un errore sconosciuto durante il caricamento dei componenti del [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-147">An unknown error occurred loading [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) components.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-148">eseguendo una delle operazioni seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-148">Take one of the following actions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-149">Contattare il [supporto tecnico Microsoft](https://support.microsoft.com/oas/default.aspx?prid=15832). Selezionare **Strumenti di sviluppo** e quindi **ASP.NET Core**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-149">Contact [Microsoft Support](https://support.microsoft.com/oas/default.aspx?prid=15832) (select **Developer Tools** then **ASP.NET Core**).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-150">Porre una domanda in Stack Overflow.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-150">Ask a question on Stack Overflow.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-151">Segnalare il problema nel [repository GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore) di ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-151">File an issue on our [GitHub repository](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore).</span></span>

### <a name="50030-in-process-startup-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-152">500.30 Errore di avvio in-process</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-152">500.30 In-Process Startup Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-153">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-153">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-154">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-154">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-155">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta di avviare .NET Core CLR in-process, ma non è possibile avviarlo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-155">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the .NET Core CLR in-process, but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-156">In genere è possibile determinare la causa di un errore di avvio del processo dalle voci nel log eventi dell'applicazione e nel log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-156">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-157">Condizioni di errore comuni:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-157">Common failure conditions:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-158">L'app non è configurata correttamente perché la destinazione è una versione di ASP.NET Core Framework condiviso che non è presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-158">The app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-159">Controllare le versioni del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core installate nel computer di destinazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-159">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-160">Utilizzando Azure Key Vault, non sono disponibili autorizzazioni per l'Key Vault.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-160">Using Azure Key Vault, lack of permissions to the Key Vault.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-161">Verificare i criteri di accesso nel Key Vault di destinazione per verificare che siano state concesse le autorizzazioni corrette.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-161">Check the access policies in the targeted Key Vault to ensure that the correct permissions are granted.</span></span>

### <a name="50031-ancm-failed-to-find-native-dependencies"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-162">500.31 ANCM Failed to Find Native Dependencies (500.31 Il modulo ASP.NET Core non è riuscito a trovare le dipendenze native)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-162">500.31 ANCM Failed to Find Native Dependencies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-163">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-163">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-164">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-164">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-165">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta di avviare il runtime di .NET Core in-process, ma non è possibile avviarlo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-165">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the .NET Core runtime in-process, but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-166">La causa più comune di questo errore di avvio è la mancata installazione del runtime di `Microsoft.NETCore.App` o di `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-166">The most common cause of this startup failure is when the `Microsoft.NETCore.App` or `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` runtime isn't installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-167">Se l'app viene distribuita per ASP.NET Core 3.0 e tale versione non esiste nel computer, si verifica questo errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-167">If the app is deployed to target ASP.NET Core 3.0 and that version doesn't exist on the machine, this error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-168">Ecco un esempio di messaggio di errore:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-168">An example error message follows:</span></span>

```
The specified framework 'Microsoft.NETCore.App', version '3.0.0' was not found.
  - The following frameworks were found:
      2.2.1 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview5-27626-15 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27713-13 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27714-15 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
      3.0.0-preview6-27723-08 at [C:\Program Files\dotnet\x64\shared\Microsoft.NETCore.App]
```

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-169">Il messaggio di errore elenca tutte le versioni di .NET Core installate e la versione richiesta dall'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-169">The error message lists all the installed .NET Core versions and the version requested by the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-170">Per correggere l'errore, eseguire una delle operazioni seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-170">To fix this error, either:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-171">Installare la versione appropriata di .NET Core nel computer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-171">Install the appropriate version of .NET Core on the machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-172">Modificare l'app in modo che usi una versione di .NET Core presente nel computer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-172">Change the app to target a version of .NET Core that's present on the machine.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-173">Pubblicare l'app come [distribuzione autonoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-173">Publish the app as a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-174">Durante l'esecuzione in fase di sviluppo (con la variabile di ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` impostata su `Development`), l'errore specifico viene scritto nella risposta HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-174">When running in development (the `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` environment variable is set to `Development`), the specific error is written to the HTTP response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-175">La causa di un errore di avvio del processo è disponibile anche nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-175">The cause of a process startup failure is also found in the Application Event Log.</span></span>

### <a name="50032-ancm-failed-to-load-dll"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-176">500.32 ANCM Failed to Load dll (500.32 Il modulo ASP.NET Core non è riuscito a caricare la DLL)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-176">500.32 ANCM Failed to Load dll</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-177">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-177">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-178">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-178">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-179">La causa più comune di questo errore è la pubblicazione dell'app per processori con architettura non compatibile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-179">The most common cause for this error is that the app is published for an incompatible processor architecture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-180">Se il processo di lavoro è in esecuzione come app a 32 bit e l'app è stata pubblicata per un'architettura a 64 bit, si verifica questo errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-180">If the worker process is running as a 32-bit app and the app was published to target 64-bit, this error occurs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-181">Per correggere l'errore, eseguire una delle operazioni seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-181">To fix this error, either:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-182">Ripubblicare l'app per processori con la stessa architettura del processo di lavoro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-182">Republish the app for the same processor architecture as the worker process.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="b43de-183">Pubblicare l'app come [distribuzione dipendente dal framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-executables-fde).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-183">Publish the app as a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-executables-fde).</span></span>

### <a name="50033-ancm-request-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-184">500.33 ANCM Request Handler Load Failure (500.33 Errore di caricamento del gestore della richiesta del modulo ASP.Net Core)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-184">500.33 ANCM Request Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-185">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-185">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-186">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-186">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-187">L'app non fa riferimento al framework `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-187">The app didn't reference the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-188">Solo le app destinate al `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` Framework possono essere ospitate dal [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-188">Only apps targeting the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework can be hosted by the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-189">Per correggere questo errore, verificare che l'app sia destinata al framework `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-189">To fix this error, confirm that the app is targeting the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App` framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-190">Controllare il framework di destinazione dell'app nel file `.runtimeconfig.json`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-190">Check the `.runtimeconfig.json` to verify the framework targeted by the app.</span></span>

### <a name="50034-ancm-mixed-hosting-models-not-supported"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-191">500.34 ANCM Mixed Hosting Models Not Supported (500.34 Modelli di hosting misto non supportati nel modulo ASP.NET Core)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-191">500.34 ANCM Mixed Hosting Models Not Supported</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-192">Il processo di lavoro non è in grado di eseguire un'app In-Process e un'app Out-of-process nello stesso processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-192">The worker process can't run both an in-process app and an out-of-process app in the same process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-193">Per correggere questo errore, eseguire le app in pool di applicazioni IIS separati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-193">To fix this error, run apps in separate IIS application pools.</span></span>

### <a name="50035-ancm-multiple-in-process-applications-in-same-process"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-194">500.35 ANCM Multiple In-Process Applications in same Process (500.35 Modulo ASP.NET Core: più applicazioni In-Process nello stesso processo)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-194">500.35 ANCM Multiple In-Process Applications in same Process</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-195">Il processo di lavoro non può eseguire più app in-process nello stesso processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-195">The worker process can't run multiple in-process apps in the same process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-196">Per correggere questo errore, eseguire le app in pool di applicazioni IIS separati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-196">To fix this error, run apps in separate IIS application pools.</span></span>

### <a name="50036-ancm-out-of-process-handler-load-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-197">500.36 ANCM Out-Of-Process Handler Load Failure (500.36 Modulo ASP.NET Core: Errore di caricamento del gestore Out-of-process)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-197">500.36 ANCM Out-Of-Process Handler Load Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-198">Il gestore delle richieste Out-of-process, *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll*, non è accanto al file *aspnetcorev2.dll*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-198">The out-of-process request handler, *aspnetcorev2_outofprocess.dll*, isn't next to the *aspnetcorev2.dll* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-199">Indica un'installazione danneggiata del [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-199">This indicates a corrupted installation of the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-200">Per correggere questo errore, riparare l'installazione del [bundle di hosting di .NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle) (per IIS) o di Visual Studio (per IIS Express).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-200">To fix this error, repair the installation of the [.NET Core Hosting Bundle](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle) (for IIS) or Visual Studio (for IIS Express).</span></span>

### <a name="50037-ancm-failed-to-start-within-startup-time-limit"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-201">500.37 ANCM Failed to Start Within Startup Time Limit (500.37 Avvio del modulo ASP.NET Core non riuscito entro il limite di tempo stabilito)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-201">500.37 ANCM Failed to Start Within Startup Time Limit</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-202">MODULO ASP.NET Core non è stato avviato entro il limite di tempo di avvio specificato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-202">ANCM failed to start within the provided startup time limit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-203">Per impostazione predefinita, il timeout è di 120 secondi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-203">By default, the timeout is 120 seconds.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-204">Questo errore può verificarsi quando si avvia un numero elevato di app nello stesso computer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-204">This error can occur when starting a large number of apps on the same machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-205">Controllare i picchi di utilizzo della CPU e della memoria nel server durante l'avvio.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-205">Check for CPU/Memory usage spikes on the server during startup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-206">Può essere necessario scaglionare il processo di avvio di più app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-206">You may need to stagger the startup process of multiple apps.</span></span>

### <a name="50038-ancm-application-dll-not-found"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-207">500,38 DLL applicazione modulo ASP.NET Core non trovata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-207">500.38 ANCM Application DLL Not Found</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-208">MODULO ASP.NET Core non è riuscito a individuare la DLL dell'applicazione, che deve essere accanto all'eseguibile.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-208">ANCM failed to locate the application DLL, which should be next to the executable.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-209">Questo errore si verifica quando si ospita un'app in pacchetto come file [eseguibile di un singolo file](/dotnet/core/whats-new/dotnet-core-3-0#single-file-executables) usando il modello di hosting in-process.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-209">This error occurs when hosting an app packaged as a [single-file executable](/dotnet/core/whats-new/dotnet-core-3-0#single-file-executables) using the in-process hosting model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-210">Il modello in-process richiede che modulo ASP.NET Core carichi l'app .NET Core nel processo IIS esistente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-210">The in-process model requires that the ANCM load the .NET Core app into the existing IIS process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-211">Questo scenario non è supportato dal modello di distribuzione a file singolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-211">This scenario isn't supported by the single-file deployment model.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-212">Per correggere l'errore, usare **uno** degli approcci seguenti nel file di progetto dell'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-212">Use **one** of the following approaches in the app's project file to fix this error:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-213">Disabilitare la pubblicazione su file singolo impostando la `PublishSingleFile` Proprietà MSBuild su `false` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-213">Disable single-file publishing by setting the `PublishSingleFile` MSBuild property to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-214">Passare al modello di hosting out-of-process impostando la `AspNetCoreHostingModel` Proprietà MSBuild su `OutOfProcess` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-214">Switch to the out-of-process hosting model by setting the `AspNetCoreHostingModel` MSBuild property to `OutOfProcess`.</span></span>

### <a name="5025-process-failure"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-215">502.5 Process Failure (Errore del processo)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-215">502.5 Process Failure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-216">Il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-216">The worker process fails.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-217">L'app non viene avviata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-217">The app doesn't start.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-218">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) tenta di avviare il processo di lavoro, ma l'avvio non riesce.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-218">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) attempts to start the worker process but it fails to start.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-219">In genere è possibile determinare la causa di un errore di avvio del processo dalle voci nel log eventi dell'applicazione e nel log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-219">The cause of a process startup failure can usually be determined from entries in the Application Event Log and the ASP.NET Core Module stdout log.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-220">Una condizione di errore comune è dovuta alla configurazione non corretta dell'app perché come destinazione viene specificata una versione del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core, che non è presente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-220">A common failure condition is the app is misconfigured due to targeting a version of the ASP.NET Core shared framework that isn't present.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-221">Controllare le versioni del framework condiviso ASP.NET Core installate nel computer di destinazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-221">Check which versions of the ASP.NET Core shared framework are installed on the target machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-222">Il *framework condiviso* è il set di assembly (file *DLL*) che vengono installati nel computer e cui fa riferimento un metapacchetto, ad esempio `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-222">The *shared framework* is the set of assemblies (*.dll* files) that are installed on the machine and referenced by a metapackage such as `Microsoft.AspNetCore.App`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-223">Il riferimento del metapacchetto può specificare una versione minima richiesta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-223">The metapackage reference can specify a minimum required version.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-224">Per altre informazioni, vedere [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/) (Il framework condiviso).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-224">For more information, see [The shared framework](https://natemcmaster.com/blog/2018/08/29/netcore-primitives-2/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-225">La pagina di errore *502.5 Errore del processo* viene restituita quando il processo di lavoro ha esito negativo a causa di un errore di configurazione dell'hosting o dell'app:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-225">The *502.5 Process Failure* error page is returned when a hosting or app misconfiguration causes the worker process to fail:</span></span>

### <a name="failed-to-start-application-errorcode-0x800700c1"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-226">Non è stato possibile avviare l'aggiornamento dell'applicazione. Errore: 0x800700c1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-226">Failed to start application (ErrorCode '0x800700c1')</span></span>

```
EventID: 1010
Source: IIS AspNetCore Module V2
Failed to start application '/LM/W3SVC/6/ROOT/', ErrorCode '0x800700c1'.
```

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-227">L'app non è stata avviata perché non è stato possibile caricarne l'assembly (*.dll*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-227">The app failed to start because the app's assembly (*.dll*) couldn't be loaded.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-228">Questo errore si verifica quando è presente una mancata corrispondenza del numero di bit tra l'app pubblicata e il processo w3wp/iisexpress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-228">This error occurs when there's a bitness mismatch between the published app and the w3wp/iisexpress process.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-229">Verificare che l'impostazione del pool di app a 32 bit sia corretta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-229">Confirm that the app pool's 32-bit setting is correct:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-230">Selezionare il pool di app in **Pool di applicazioni** di Gestione IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-230">Select the app pool in IIS Manager's **Application Pools**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-231">Selezionare **Impostazioni avanzate** in **Modifica pool di applicazioni** nel pannello **Azioni**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-231">Select **Advanced Settings** under **Edit Application Pool** in the **Actions** panel.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-232">Impostare **Attiva applicazioni a 32 bit**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-232">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications**:</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-233">Se si sta sviluppando un'app a 32 bit (x86), impostare il valore su `True`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-233">If deploying a 32-bit (x86) app, set the value to `True`.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-234">Se si sta sviluppando un'app a 64 bit (x64), impostare il valore su `False`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-234">If deploying a 64-bit (x64) app, set the value to `False`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-235">Verificare che non esista un conflitto tra una `<Platform>` proprietà di MSBuild nel file di progetto e il bit pubblicato dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-235">Confirm that there isn't a conflict between a `<Platform>` MSBuild property in the project file and the published bitness of the app.</span></span>

### <a name="connection-reset"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-236">Connection reset (Connessione ripristinata)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-236">Connection reset</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-237">Se si verifica un errore dopo l'invio delle intestazioni, è troppo tardi perché il server possa inviare un codice **500 Errore interno del server** quando si verifica un errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-237">If an error occurs after the headers are sent, it's too late for the server to send a **500 Internal Server Error** when an error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-238">Questo spesso accade quando si verifica un errore durante la serializzazione di oggetti complessi per una risposta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-238">This often happens when an error occurs during the serialization of complex objects for a response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-239">Questo tipo di errore viene visualizzato come un errore di *reimpostazione della connessione* nel client.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-239">This type of error appears as a *connection reset* error on the client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-240">La [registrazione delle applicazioni](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) può consentire di risolvere questi tipi di errori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-240">[Application logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) can help troubleshoot these types of errors.</span></span>

### <a name="default-startup-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-241">Limiti di avvio predefiniti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-241">Default startup limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-242">Il [modulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) è configurato con un valore predefinito di *startupTimeLimit* di 120 secondi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-242">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) is configured with a default *startupTimeLimit* of 120 seconds.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-243">Quando si mantiene il valore predefinito, l'avvio di un'app potrebbe richiedere fino a due minuti prima che il modulo registri un errore del processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-243">When left at the default value, an app may take up to two minutes to start before the module logs a process failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-244">Per informazioni sulla configurazione del modulo, vedere [Attributi dell'elemento aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-244">For information on configuring the module, see [Attributes of the aspNetCore element](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#attributes-of-the-aspnetcore-element).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-245">Risolvere i problemi relativi al servizio app Azure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-245">Troubleshoot on Azure App Service</span></span>

[!INCLUDE [Azure App Service Preview Notice](~/includes/azure-apps-preview-notice.md)]

### <a name="application-event-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-246">Registro eventi applicazioni (servizio app Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-246">Application Event Log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-247">Per accedere al log eventi dell'applicazione, usare il pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** nel portale di Azure:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-247">To access the Application Event Log, use the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-248">Nel portale di Azure aprire l'app in **Servizi app**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-248">In the Azure portal, open the app in **App Services**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-249">Selezionare **Diagnostica e risoluzione dei problemi**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-249">Select **Diagnose and solve problems**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-250">Selezionare l'intestazione **Strumenti di diagnostica**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-250">Select the **Diagnostic Tools** heading.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-251">In **Strumenti di supporto** selezionare il pulsante **Eventi dell'applicazione**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-251">Under **Support Tools**, select the **Application Events** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-252">Esaminare l'errore più recente dalla voce *IIS AspNetCoreModule* o *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* nella colonna **Origine**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-252">Examine the latest error provided by the *IIS AspNetCoreModule* or *IIS AspNetCoreModule V2* entry in the **Source** column.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-253">Un'alternativa all'uso del pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** consiste nell'esaminare direttamente il file del log eventi dell'applicazione usando [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-253">An alternative to using the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade is to examine the Application Event Log file directly using [Kudu](https://github.com/projectkudu/kudu/wiki):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-254">Aprire **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **Strumenti di sviluppo**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-254">Open **Advanced Tools** in the **Development Tools** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-255">Selezionare il **pulsante &rarr; Vai** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-255">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-256">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-256">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-257">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-257">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-258">Aprire la cartella **LogFiles** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-258">Open the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-259">Selezionare l'icona della matita accanto al file *eventlog.xml*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-259">Select the pencil icon next to the *eventlog.xml* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-260">Esaminare il log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-260">Examine the log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-261">Scorrere fino alla fine del log per visualizzare gli eventi più recenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-261">Scroll to the bottom of the log to see the most recent events.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-in-the-kudu-console"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-262">Eseguire l'app nella console Kudu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-262">Run the app in the Kudu console</span></span>

#### <a name="test-a-32-bit-x86-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-269">Test di un'app a 32 bit (x86)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-269">Test a 32-bit (x86) app</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-292">Log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core (servizio app Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-292">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-293">La mancata disabilitazione del log stdout può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-293">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-294">Non esiste alcun limite per le dimensioni dei file di log o il numero di file di log che è possibile creare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-294">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-295">Usare la registrazione stdout solo per la risoluzione dei problemi di avvio delle app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-295">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-296">Per la registrazione generale in un'app ASP.NET Core dopo l'avvio, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-296">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-297">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-297">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-298">Il log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core spesso registra utili messaggi di errore non disponibili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-298">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-299">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-299">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-300">Nel portale di Azure passare all'app Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-300">In the Azure Portal, navigate to the web app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-301">Nel pannello **servizio app** immettere **Kudu** nella casella di ricerca.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-301">In the **App Service** blade, enter **kudu** in the search box.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-302">Selezionare **strumenti avanzati** > **Vai**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-302">Select **Advanced Tools** > **Go**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-303">Selezionare  **console di Debug > cmd**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-303">Select  **Debug console > CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-304">Passa a *sito/wwwroot*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-304">Navigate to *site/wwwroot*</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-305">Selezionare l'icona a matita per modificare il file di *web.config* .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-305">Select the pencil icon to edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-306">Nell' `<aspNetCore />` elemento impostare `stdoutLogEnabled="true"` e selezionare **Salva**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-306">In the `<aspNetCore />` element, set `stdoutLogEnabled="true"` and select **Save**.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-307">Disabilitare la registrazione stdout quando la risoluzione dei problemi è stata completata impostando `stdoutLogEnabled="false"` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-307">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete by setting `stdoutLogEnabled="false"`.</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-315">Aggiungere le impostazioni `<handlerSettings>` indicate in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) al file *web.config* dell'app distribuita, usando la console Kudu:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-315">Add the `<handlerSettings>` shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to the live app's *web.config* file using the Kudu console:</span></span>

     1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-320">Aprire le cartelle nel **sito** del percorso  >  **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-320">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-321">Modificare il file *web.config* selezionando il pulsante a forma di matita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-321">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-322">Aggiungere la sezione `<handlerSettings>` come illustrato in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-322">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-323">Fare clic sul pulsante **Salva**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-323">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>
