<span data-ttu-id="b43de-627">L'output della console dall'app, che visualizza gli eventuali errori, viene inviato tramite pipe alla console Kudu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-627">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is piped to the Kudu console.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-628">Log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core (servizio app Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-628">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-629">Il log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core spesso registra utili messaggi di errore non disponibili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-629">The ASP.NET Core Module stdout log often records useful error messages not found in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-630">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-630">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-631">Passare al pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** nel portale di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-631">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-632">In **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY** (SELEZIONARE LA CATEGORIA DEL PROBLEMA) selezionare il pulsante **Web App Down** (App Web inattiva).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-632">Under **SELECT PROBLEM CATEGORY**, select the **Web App Down** button.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-633">In **Suggested Solutions (Soluzioni consigliate)** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection** (Abilita il reindirizzamento del log Stdout) selezionare il pulsante **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config** (Apri la console Kudu per modificare Web.Config).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-633">Under **Suggested Solutions** > **Enable Stdout Log Redirection**, select the button to **Open Kudu Console to edit Web.Config**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-634">Nella **console diagnostica** Kudu aprire le cartelle nel percorso **site** > **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-634">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-635">Scorrere verso il basso fino a visualizzare il file *web.config* in fondo all'elenco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-635">Scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-636">Fare clic sull'icona della matita accanto al file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-636">Click the pencil icon next to the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-637">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `true` e cambiare il percorso di **stdoutLogFile** in: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-637">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to: `\\?\%home%\LogFiles\stdout`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-638">Selezionare **Salva** per salvare il file *web.config* aggiornato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-638">Select **Save** to save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-639">Effettuare una richiesta all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-639">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-640">Tornare al portale di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-640">Return to the Azure portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-641">Selezionare il pannello **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **STRUMENTI DI SVILUPPO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-641">Select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-642">Selezionare il **pulsante &rarr; Vai** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-642">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-643">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-643">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-644">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-644">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-645">Selezionare la cartella **LogFiles**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-645">Select the **LogFiles** folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-646">Controllare la colonna **Data modifica** e selezionare l'icona della matita per modificare il log stdout con la data di modifica più recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-646">Inspect the **Modified** column and select the pencil icon to edit the stdout log with the latest modification date.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-647">Quando si apre il file di log, verrà visualizzato l'errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-647">When the log file opens, the error is displayed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-648">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, disabilitare la registrazione stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-648">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-649">Nella **console diagnostica** Kudu tornare al percorso **site** > **wwwroot** per visualizzare il file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-649">In the Kudu **Diagnostic Console**, return to the path **site** > **wwwroot** to reveal the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-650">Aprire nuovamente il file **web.config** selezionando l'icona della matita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-650">Open the **web.config** file again by selecting the pencil icon.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-651">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-651">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-652">Selezionare **Salva** per salvare il file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-652">Select **Save** to save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-653">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-653">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-654">La mancata disabilitazione del log stdout può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-654">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-655">Non esiste alcun limite per le dimensioni dei file di log o il numero di file di log che è possibile creare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-655">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-656">Usare la registrazione stdout solo per la risoluzione dei problemi di avvio delle app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-656">Only use stdout logging to troubleshoot app startup problems.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-657">Per la registrazione generale in un'app ASP.NET Core dopo l'avvio, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-657">For general logging in an ASP.NET Core app after startup, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-658">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-658">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-azure-app-service"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-659">Log di debug del modulo ASP.NET Core (servizio app Azure)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-659">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (Azure App Service)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-660">Il log di debug del modulo ASP.NET Core fornisce dati di registrazione aggiuntivi e più approfonditi dal modulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-660">The ASP.NET Core Module debug log provides additional, deeper logging from the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-661">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-661">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-663">Seguire le istruzioni in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) per configurare l'app per la registrazione di diagnostica avanzata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-663">Follow the instructions in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to configure the app for an enhanced diagnostic logging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-664">Ridistribuire l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-664">Redeploy the app.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-665">Aggiungere le impostazioni `<handlerSettings>` indicate in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) al file *web.config* dell'app distribuita, usando la console Kudu:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-665">Add the `<handlerSettings>` shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs) to the live app's *web.config* file using the Kudu console:</span></span>

     1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-670">Aprire le cartelle nel **sito** del percorso  >  **wwwroot**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-670">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-671">Modificare il file *web.config* selezionando il pulsante a forma di matita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-671">Edit the *web.config* file by selecting the pencil button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-672">Aggiungere la sezione `<handlerSettings>` come illustrato in [Log di diagnostica avanzati](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-672">Add the `<handlerSettings>` section as shown in [Enhanced diagnostic logs](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-673">Fare clic sul pulsante **Salva**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-673">Select the **Save** button.</span></span>

### <a name="monitoring-blades"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-697">Pannelli di monitoraggio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-697">Monitoring blades</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-698">I pannelli di monitoraggio forniscono un'esperienza di risoluzione dei problemi alternativa ai metodi descritti in precedenza in questo argomento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-698">Monitoring blades provide an alternative troubleshooting experience to the methods described earlier in the topic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-699">È possibile usare questi pannelli per diagnosticare gli errori della serie 500.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-699">These blades can be used to diagnose 500-series errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-700">Verificare che le estensioni di ASP.NET Core siano installate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-700">Confirm that the ASP.NET Core Extensions are installed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-701">Se le estensioni non sono installate, installarle manualmente:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-701">If the extensions aren't installed, install them manually:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-705">Scegliere **ASP.NET Core Extensions** (Estensioni ASP.NET Core) dall'elenco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-705">Choose the **ASP.NET Core Extensions** from the list.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-706">Selezionare **OK** per accettare le condizioni legali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-706">Select **OK** to accept the legal terms.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-709">Se la registrazione stdout non è abilitata, attenersi ai passaggi riportati di seguito:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-709">If stdout logging isn't enabled, follow these steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-710">Nel portale di Azure selezionare il pannello **Strumenti avanzati** nell'area **STRUMENTI DI SVILUPPO**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-710">In the Azure portal, select the **Advanced Tools** blade in the **DEVELOPMENT TOOLS** area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-711">Selezionare il **pulsante &rarr; Vai** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-711">Select the **Go&rarr;** button.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-712">Verrà aperta la console Kudu in una nuova scheda o finestra del browser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-712">The Kudu console opens in a new browser tab or window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-713">Usando la barra di spostamento nella parte superiore della pagina, aprire **Console di debug** e selezionare **CMD**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-713">Using the navigation bar at the top of the page, open **Debug console** and select **CMD**.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-714">Aprire le cartelle nel percorso **site** > **wwwroot** e scorrere verso il basso fino a visualizzare il file *web.config* in fondo all'elenco.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-714">Open the folders to the path **site** > **wwwroot** and scroll down to reveal the *web.config* file at the bottom of the list.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-718">Passare all'attivazione della registrazione diagnostica:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-718">Proceed to activate diagnostic logging:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-722">Per includere la traccia delle richieste non riuscite, anche nota come registrazione FREB (Failed Request Event Buffering), selezionare l'interruttore **Attivato** per **Traccia delle richieste non riuscite**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-722">To include failed request tracing, also known as Failed Request Event Buffering (FREB) logging, select the **On** switch for **Failed request tracing**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-724">Effettuare una richiesta all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-724">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-725">Nei dati del flusso di registrazione viene indicata la causa dell'errore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-725">Within the log stream data, the cause of the error is indicated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-726">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, assicurarsi di disabilitare la registrazione stdout.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-726">Be sure to disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-727">Per visualizzare i log di traccia delle richieste non riuscite (log FREB):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-727">To view the failed request tracing logs (FREB logs):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-728">Passare al pannello **Diagnostica e risolvi i problemi** nel portale di Azure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-728">Navigate to the **Diagnose and solve problems** blade in the Azure portal.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-729">Selezionare **Failed Request Tracing Logs** (Log di traccia delle richieste non riuscite) nell'area **STRUMENTI DI SUPPORTO** della barra laterale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-729">Select **Failed Request Tracing Logs** from the **SUPPORT TOOLS** area of the sidebar.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-730">Per altre informazioni, vedere la [sezione relativa alla traccia delle richieste non riuscite nell'argomento Abilitare la registrazione diagnostica per le app Web nel servizio app di Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) e [Domande frequenti sulle prestazioni delle applicazioni in App Web di Azure: Come si abilita la traccia delle richieste non riuscite?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-730">See [Failed request traces section of the Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service topic](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log#failed-request-traces) and the [Application performance FAQs for Web Apps in Azure: How do I turn on failed request tracing?](/azure/app-service/app-service-web-availability-performance-application-issues-faq#how-do-i-turn-on-failed-request-tracing) for more information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-731">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Abilitare la registrazione diagnostica per le app Web nel servizio app di Azure](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-731">For more information, see [Enable diagnostics logging for web apps in Azure App Service](/azure/app-service/web-sites-enable-diagnostic-log).</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-734">Per la registrazione di routine in un'app ASP.NET Core, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-734">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-735">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-735">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

## <a name="troubleshoot-on-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-736">Risolvere i problemi in IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-736">Troubleshoot on IIS</span></span>

### <a name="application-event-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-737">Registro eventi applicazioni (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-737">Application Event Log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-738">Accedere al log eventi dell'applicazione:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-738">Access the Application Event Log:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-739">Aprire il menu Start, cercare *Visualizzatore eventi* e selezionare l'app **Visualizzatore eventi** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-739">Open the Start menu, search for *Event Viewer*, and select the **Event Viewer** app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-740">In **Visualizzatore eventi** aprire il nodo **Registri di Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-740">In **Event Viewer**, open the **Windows Logs** node.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-741">Selezionare **Applicazione** per aprire il log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-741">Select **Application** to open the Application Event Log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-742">Cercare gli errori associati all'app in cui si è verificato il problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-742">Search for errors associated with the failing app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-743">Gli errori presentano un valore *Modulo AspNetCore IIS* o *Modulo AspNetCore IIS Express* nella colonna *Origine*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-743">Errors have a value of *IIS AspNetCore Module* or *IIS Express AspNetCore Module* in the *Source* column.</span></span>

### <a name="run-the-app-at-a-command-prompt"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-744">Eseguire l'app da un prompt dei comandi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-744">Run the app at a command prompt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-745">Molti errori di avvio non producono informazioni utili nel log eventi dell'applicazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-745">Many startup errors don't produce useful information in the Application Event Log.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-746">È possibile individuare la causa di alcuni errori eseguendo l'app da un prompt dei comandi nel sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-746">You can find the cause of some errors by running the app at a command prompt on the hosting system.</span></span>

#### <a name="framework-dependent-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-747">Distribuzione dipendente dal framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-747">Framework-dependent deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-748">Se l'app è una [distribuzione dipendente dal framework](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-748">If the app is a [framework-dependent deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#framework-dependent-deployments-fdd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-749">Da un prompt dei comandi passare alla cartella di distribuzione e avviare l'app eseguendo l'assembly dell'app con *dotnet.exe*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-749">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app by executing the app's assembly with *dotnet.exe*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-750">Nel comando seguente sostituire il nome dell'assembly dell'app per \<assembly_name> : `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-750">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `dotnet .\<assembly_name>.dll`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-751">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà scritto nella finestra della console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-751">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-752">Se gli errori si verificano quando si effettua una richiesta all'app, effettuare una richiesta all'host e alla porta su cui è in ascolto Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-752">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-753">Usando l'host e la porta predefiniti, effettuare una richiesta a `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-753">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-754">Se l'app risponde normalmente nell'indirizzo endpoint di Kestrel, è più probabile che il problema sia associato alla configurazione dell'host e che non sia interno all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-754">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

#### <a name="self-contained-deployment"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-755">Distribuzione autonoma</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-755">Self-contained deployment</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-756">Se l'app è una [distribuzione autonoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-756">If the app is a [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-757">Da un prompt dei comandi passare alla cartella di distribuzione e avviare il file eseguibile dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-757">At a command prompt, navigate to the deployment folder and run the app's executable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-758">Nel comando seguente sostituire il nome dell'assembly dell'app per \<assembly_name> : `<assembly_name>.exe` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-758">In the following command, substitute the name of the app's assembly for \<assembly_name>: `<assembly_name>.exe`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-759">L'output della console per l'app, in cui sono indicati gli eventuali errori, verrà scritto nella finestra della console.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-759">The console output from the app, showing any errors, is written to the console window.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-760">Se gli errori si verificano quando si effettua una richiesta all'app, effettuare una richiesta all'host e alla porta su cui è in ascolto Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-760">If the errors occur when making a request to the app, make a request to the host and port where Kestrel listens.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-761">Usando l'host e la porta predefiniti, effettuare una richiesta a `http://localhost:5000/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-761">Using the default host and post, make a request to `http://localhost:5000/`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-762">Se l'app risponde normalmente nell'indirizzo endpoint di Kestrel, è più probabile che il problema sia associato alla configurazione dell'host e che non sia interno all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-762">If the app responds normally at the Kestrel endpoint address, the problem is more likely related to the hosting configuration and less likely within the app.</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-stdout-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-763">Log stdout del modulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-763">ASP.NET Core Module stdout log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-764">Per abilitare e visualizzare i log stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-764">To enable and view stdout logs:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-765">Passare alla cartella di distribuzione del sito nel sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-765">Navigate to the site's deployment folder on the hosting system.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-766">Se la cartella *logs* non è presente, creare la cartella.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-766">If the *logs* folder isn't present, create the folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-767">Per istruzioni su come impostare MSBuild per la creazione automatica della cartella *logs* nella distribuzione, vedere l'argomento [Struttura della directory](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-767">For instructions on how to enable MSBuild to create the *logs* folder in the deployment automatically, see the [Directory structure](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure) topic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-768">Modificare il file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-768">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-769">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `true` e modificare il percorso di **stdoutLogFile** in modo da fare riferimento alla cartella *logs*, ad esempio `.\logs\stdout`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-769">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `true` and change the **stdoutLogFile** path to point to the *logs* folder (for example, `.\logs\stdout`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-770">`stdout` nel percorso è il prefisso del nome del file di log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-770">`stdout` in the path is the log file name prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-771">Un timestamp, l'ID del processo e l'estensione del file vengono aggiunti automaticamente al momento della creazione del log.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-771">A timestamp, process id, and file extension are added automatically when the log is created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-772">Usando `stdout` come prefisso del nome del file, un tipico file di log è denominato *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-772">Using `stdout` as the file name prefix, a typical log file is named *stdout_20180205184032_5412.log*.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-773">Assicurarsi che l'identità del pool di applicazioni disponga delle autorizzazioni di scrittura per la cartella *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-773">Ensure your application pool's identity has write permissions to the *logs* folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-774">Salvare il file *web.config* aggiornato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-774">Save the updated *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-775">Effettuare una richiesta all'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-775">Make a request to the app.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-776">Passare alla cartella *logs*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-776">Navigate to the *logs* folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-777">Trovare e aprire il log stdout più recente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-777">Find and open the most recent stdout log.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-778">Esaminare il log per verificare se sono presenti errori.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-778">Study the log for errors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-779">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, disabilitare la registrazione stdout:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-779">Disable stdout logging when troubleshooting is complete:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-780">Modificare il file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-780">Edit the *web.config* file.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-781">Impostare **stdoutLogEnabled** su `false`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-781">Set **stdoutLogEnabled** to `false`.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-782">Salvare il file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-782">Save the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-783">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-783">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#log-creation-and-redirection>.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-784">La mancata disabilitazione del log stdout può causare un errore dell'app o del server.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-784">Failure to disable the stdout log can lead to app or server failure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-785">Non esiste alcun limite per le dimensioni dei file di log o il numero di file di log che è possibile creare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-785">There's no limit on log file size or the number of log files created.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-786">Per la registrazione di routine in un'app ASP.NET Core, usare una libreria di registrazione che limita le dimensioni dei file di log e ne esegue la rotazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-786">For routine logging in an ASP.NET Core app, use a logging library that limits log file size and rotates logs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-787">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Provider di registrazione di terze parti](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-787">For more information, see [third-party logging providers](xref:fundamentals/logging/index#third-party-logging-providers).</span></span>

### <a name="aspnet-core-module-debug-log-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-788">Log di debug del modulo ASP.NET Core (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-788">ASP.NET Core Module debug log (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-789">Aggiungere le impostazioni del gestore seguenti al file di *web.config* dell'app per abilitare ASP.NET Core log di debug del modulo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-789">Add the following handler settings to the app's *web.config* file to enable ASP.NET Core Module debug log:</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore ...>
  <handlerSettings>
    <handlerSetting name="debugLevel" value="file" />
    <handlerSetting name="debugFile" value="c:\temp\ancm.log" />
  </handlerSettings>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-790">Verificare che il percorso specificato per il log esista e che l'identità del pool di applicazioni abbia le autorizzazioni di scrittura nel percorso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-790">Confirm that the path specified for the log exists and that the app pool's identity has write permissions to the location.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-791">Per altre informazioni, vedere <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-791">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#enhanced-diagnostic-logs>.</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-developer-exception-page"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-792">Abilitare la pagina delle eccezioni per gli sviluppatori</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-792">Enable the Developer Exception Page</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-793">La variabile di ambiente `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [ può essere aggiunta a web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) per eseguire l'app nell'ambiente di sviluppo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-793">The `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` [environment variable can be added to web.config](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables) to run the app in the Development environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-794">Purché l'ambiente non sia sottoposto a override durante l'avvio dell'app tramite `UseEnvironment` nel generatore di host, l'impostazione della variabile di ambiente consente di visualizzare la [pagina delle eccezioni per gli sviluppatori](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) quando viene eseguita l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-794">As long as the environment isn't overridden in app startup by `UseEnvironment` on the host builder, setting the environment variable allows the [Developer Exception Page](xref:fundamentals/error-handling) to appear when the app is run.</span></span>

```xml
<aspNetCore processPath="dotnet"
      arguments=".\MyApp.dll"
      stdoutLogEnabled="false"
      stdoutLogFile=".\logs\stdout"
      hostingModel="InProcess">
  <environmentVariables>
    <environmentVariable name="ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT" value="Development" />
  </environmentVariables>
</aspNetCore>
```

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-795">L'impostazione della variabile di ambiente per `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` è consigliata solo per l'uso in server di gestione temporanea e test non esposti a Internet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-795">Setting the environment variable for `ASPNETCORE_ENVIRONMENT` is only recommended for use on staging and testing servers that aren't exposed to the Internet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-796">Al termine della risoluzione dei problemi, rimuovere la variabile di ambiente dal file *web.config*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-796">Remove the environment variable from the *web.config* file after troubleshooting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-797">Per informazioni sull'impostazione delle variabili di ambiente in *web.config*, vedere [elemento figlio environmentVariables di aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-797">For information on setting environment variables in *web.config*, see [environmentVariables child element of aspNetCore](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#setting-environment-variables).</span></span>

### <a name="obtain-data-from-an-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-798">Ottenere dati da un'app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-798">Obtain data from an app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-799">Se un'app è in grado di rispondere alle richieste, è possibile ottenere dati sulle richieste, le connessioni e altri dati dall'app tramite middleware inline di terminale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-799">If an app is capable of responding to requests, obtain request, connection, and additional data from the app using terminal inline middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-800">Per altre informazioni e codice di esempio, vedere <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-800">For more information and sample code, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#obtain-data-from-an-app>.</span></span>

### <a name="slow-or-hanging-app-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-801">App lenta o sospesa (IIS)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-801">Slow or hanging app (IIS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-802">Un *dump di arresto anomalo* del sistema è uno snapshot della memoria del sistema e può contribuire a determinare la provocazione di un arresto anomalo dell'app, dell'avvio o dell'applicazione lenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-802">A *crash dump* is a snapshot of the system's memory and can help determine the cause of an app crash, startup failure, or slow app.</span></span>

#### <a name="app-crashes-or-encounters-an-exception"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-803">Arresto anomalo o eccezione di un'app</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-803">App crashes or encounters an exception</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-804">Ottenere e analizzare un dump da [Segnalazione errori Windows](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-804">Obtain and analyze a dump from [Windows Error Reporting (WER)](/windows/desktop/wer/windows-error-reporting):</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-805">Creare una cartella per i file dump di arresto anomalo del sistema in `c:\dumps`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-805">Create a folder to hold crash dump files at `c:\dumps`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-806">Il pool di app deve avere accesso in scrittura alla cartella.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-806">The app pool must have write access to the folder.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-807">Eseguire lo [script di PowerShell EnableDumps](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-807">Run the [EnableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/EnableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-808">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting in-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-808">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps w3wp.exe c:\dumps
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-809">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting out-of-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-809">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\EnableDumps dotnet.exe c:\dumps
     ```

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-810">Eseguire l'app nelle condizioni che causano l'arresto anomalo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-810">Run the app under the conditions that cause the crash to occur.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-811">Dopo che si è verificato l'arresto anomalo, eseguire lo [script di PowerShell DisableDumps](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-811">After the crash has occurred, run the [DisableDumps PowerShell script](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/blob/master/aspnetcore/test/troubleshoot-azure-iis/scripts/DisableDumps.ps1):</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-812">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting in-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *w3wp.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-812">If the app uses the [in-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#in-process-hosting-model), run the script for *w3wp.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps w3wp.exe
     ```

   * <span data-ttu-id="b43de-813">Se l'app usa il [modello di hosting out-of-process](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), eseguire lo script per *dotnet.exe*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-813">If the app uses the [out-of-process hosting model](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/index#out-of-process-hosting-model), run the script for *dotnet.exe*:</span></span>

     ```console
     .\DisableDumps dotnet.exe
     ```

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-814">Dopo l'arresto anomalo di un'app e la raccolta dei dump, l'app può terminare normalmente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-814">After an app crashes and dump collection is complete, the app is allowed to terminate normally.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-815">Lo script di PowerShell configura Segnalazione errori Windows per raccogliere fino a cinque dump per ogni app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-815">The PowerShell script configures WER to collect up to five dumps per app.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-816">I dump di arresto anomalo del sistema potrebbero richiedere una grande quantità di spazio su disco (fino a diversi gigabyte ognuno).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-816">Crash dumps might take up a large amount of disk space (up to several gigabytes each).</span></span>

#### <a name="app-hangs-fails-during-startup-or-runs-normally"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-817">L'app si blocca, si verifica un errore durante l'avvio o viene eseguita normalmente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-817">App hangs, fails during startup, or runs normally</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-818">Quando un'app si *blocca* (smette di rispondere ma non si arresta in modo anomalo), si verifica un errore durante l'avvio o viene eseguita normalmente, vedere [file di dump in modalità utente: scegliere lo strumento migliore](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) per selezionare uno strumento appropriato per produrre il dump.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-818">When an app *hangs* (stops responding but doesn't crash), fails during startup, or runs normally, see [User-Mode Dump Files: Choosing the Best Tool](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/user-mode-dump-files#choosing-the-best-tool) to select an appropriate tool to produce the dump.</span></span>

#### <a name="analyze-the-dump"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-819">Analizzare il dump</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-819">Analyze the dump</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-820">È possibile analizzare un dump usando diversi approcci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-820">A dump can be analyzed using several approaches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-821">Per altre informazioni, vedere [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file) (Analisi di un file dump in modalità utente).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-821">For more information, see [Analyzing a User-Mode Dump File](/windows-hardware/drivers/debugger/analyzing-a-user-mode-dump-file).</span></span>

## <a name="clear-package-caches"></a><span data-ttu-id="b43de-822">Cancella cache di pacchetti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-822">Clear package caches</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b43de-823">Un'app funzionante potrebbe non riuscire immediatamente dopo l'aggiornamento del .NET Core SDK nel computer di sviluppo o la modifica delle versioni del pacchetto all'interno dell'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-823">A functioning app may fail immediately after upgrading either the .NET Core SDK on the development machine or changing package versions within the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-824">In alcuni casi i pacchetti incoerenti possono interrompere un'app quando si eseguono aggiornamenti principali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-824">In some cases, incoherent packages may break an app when performing major upgrades.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-825">La maggior parte di questi problemi può essere risolta attenendosi alle istruzioni seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-825">Most of these issues can be fixed by following these instructions:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-826">Eliminare le cartelle *bin* e *obj*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-826">Delete the *bin* and *obj* folders.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-827">Cancellare le cache dei pacchetti eseguendo [le impostazioni locali di DotNet NuGet All--Clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) da una shell dei comandi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-827">Clear the package caches by executing [dotnet nuget locals all --clear](/dotnet/core/tools/dotnet-nuget-locals) from a command shell.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="b43de-828">La cancellazione delle cache dei pacchetti può essere eseguita anche con lo strumento [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) e l'esecuzione del comando `nuget locals all -clear` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-828">Clearing package caches can also be accomplished with the [nuget.exe](https://www.nuget.org/downloads) tool and executing the command `nuget locals all -clear`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b43de-829">*nuget.exe* non è un'installazione inclusa con il sistema operativo desktop Windows e deve essere ottenuta separatamente dal [sito Web NuGet](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-829">*nuget.exe* isn't a bundled install with the Windows desktop operating system and must be obtained separately from the [NuGet website](https://www.nuget.org/downloads).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-830">Ripristinare e ricompilare il progetto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-830">Restore and rebuild the project.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="b43de-831">Eliminare tutti i file nella cartella di distribuzione nel server prima di ridistribuire l'app.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b43de-831">Delete all of the files in the deployment folder on the server prior to redeploying the app.</span></span>
